How we accommodate this unprecedented population growth and respond to climate change is currently the subject of vigorous political debate.\u00a0\nThe Forum's speakers will identify the key challenges of the next decades, from densification to de-growth, innovation to adaptive re-use, and help us to transform plans into decisive action.\nLiving Cities Forum in Melbourne is\u00a0supported by the Victorian Government through Creative Victoria and Development Victoria and is presented by the Naomi Milgrom Foundation in partnership with Open House Melbourne, Melbourne School of Design, Monash University, RMIT University, Australian Institute of Architects and Planning Institute of Australia.\nPlease note: Registrations open at 8am for a prompt 8.30am commencement. of positions taken.\u00a0 Penalties and interest can apply if your clients take a position that is not reasonably arguable, and advisors must inform clients of the relevant risks.\n\u00a0- Lodgement requirements for income tax returns\n\u00a0- The Commissioner's ability to amend assessments and relevant timeframes\n\u00a0- Taxpayers' ability to object to assessments, amended assessments or ruling decisions\n\u00a0- Public and Private rulings from the ATO and their impact on clients\n\u00a0- Penalties and interest arising from amended assessments\n\u00a0\nAssessable Income Fundamentals\nThe basic ordinary income provision seems simple on a base reading, but understanding whether an isolated transaction is taxed as ordinary income or statutory income (e.g. capital gains) becomes very important to our clients.\n\u00a0- Key types of ordinary income - personal exertion, property, business\n\u00a0- Isolated transactions and the potential to be taxed as ordinary income; and why it matters\n\u00a0 - Exempt income and Non-Assessable Non-Exempt Income\n\u00a0- Timing of income recognition\n\u00a0\n Allowable Deductions Fundamentals\nDeductions can seem as simple as expenses relating to business, but there is a lot more to it than a nexus to income.\n\u00a0- What is capital expenditure?\u00a0 A look at key cases that consider the matter\n\u00a0- When is expenditure private in nature?\n\u00a0- Timing of deductions, including trading stock\n\u00a0\nDay 2\nCapital Gains Tax Fundamentals\nCapital Gains Tax (CGT) has a lot more to it than determining proceeds and cost base, and new tax practitioners should be aware of what to look out for.\n\u00a0- CGT assets and separate assets\n\u00a0- Timing of capital gains for different CGT events\n\u00a0- Capital proceeds and modifications\n\u00a0- Cost base elements and modifications\n\u00a0- CGT Discounts\n\u00a0- Exemptions and anti-overlap provisions\n\u00a0\n Capital Allowances\u00a0\nAll clients will instant asset write offs for small business entities\n\nBusiness Structures\nWhen advising clients in respect of a business structure, tax is a key consideration.\u00a0\u00a0\n\u00a0- Key features of the major structure types (sole trader, partnership, trust and company)\u00a0\n\u00a0- Tax treatment of different structures\n\u00a0\nTax Reconciliations\nA key aspect of our work is taking accounting reports and adjusting relevant numbers to calculate taxable income.\u00a0 Understanding the fundamentals of accounting and the required adjustments to tax is imperative in being a valuable member of risks.</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Lodgement requirements for income tax returns</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- The Commissioner's ability to amend assessments and relevant timeframes</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Taxpayers' ability to object to assessments, amended assessments or ruling decisions</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Public and Private rulings from the ATO and their impact on clients</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Penalties and interest arising from amended assessments</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN><EM>Assessable Income Fundamentals</EM></SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>The basic ordinary income provision seems simple on a base reading, but understanding whether an isolated transaction is taxed as ordinary income or statutory income (e.g. capital gains) becomes very important to our clients.</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Key types of ordinary income - personal exertion, property, business</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Isolated transactions and the potential to be taxed as ordinary income; and why it matters</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0 - Exempt income and Non-Assessable Non-Exempt Income</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Timing of income recognition</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN> <I><SPAN>Allowable Deductions Fundamentals</SPAN></I></SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>Deductions can seem as simple as expenses relating to business, but there is a lot more to it than a nexus to income.</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- What is capital expenditure?\u00a0 A look at key cases that consider the matter</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- When is expenditure private in nature?</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Timing of deductions, including trading stock</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0</SPAN></P>\n<H3 CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><I><SPAN><SPAN>Day 2</SPAN></SPAN></I></H3>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN><I><SPAN>Capital Gains Tax Fundamentals</SPAN></I></SPAN><SPAN></SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>Capital Gains Tax (CGT) has a lot more to it than determining proceeds and cost base, and new tax practitioners should be aware of what to look out for.</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- CGT assets and separate assets</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Timing of capital gains for different CGT events</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Capital proceeds and modifications</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Cost base elements and modifications</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- CGT Discounts</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Exemptions and anti-overlap provisions</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN> <EM>Capital Allowances\u00a0</EM></SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>All clients will have fixed assets subject to tax depreciation, and identifying errors in calculations as well as spotting opportunities for faster write-offs is a benefit to clients.</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- What is a depreciating asset?</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Who holds the relevant asset?</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- How do we calculate balancing adjustments?</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- What sort of business related costs are deductible over 5 years?</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Low value pools and instant asset write offs for small business entities</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><BR></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN><EM>Business Structures</EM></SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>When advising clients in respect of a business structure, tax is a key consideration.\u00a0\u00a0</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Key features of the major structure types (sole trader, partnership, trust and company)\u00a0</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Tax treatment of different structures</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN><I><SPAN>Tax Reconciliations</SPAN></I></SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>A key aspect of our work is taking accounting reports and adjusting relevant numbers to calculate taxable income.\u00a0 Understanding the fundamentals of accounting and the required adjustments to tax is imperative in being a valuable member of the team.</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- Key adjustments from accounting to tax</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN>\u00a0- e.g. depreciation, profit/loss on disposals, leasing costs, provisions, accruals, capital raising</SPAN></P>\n<P CLASS=\"MsoNormal\"><SPAN><BR></SPAN></P>\n<P><SPAN><STRONG>4:30pm to 4:45pm</STRONG><BR><EM>Close of Workshop</EM></SPAN></P>\n<P><BR></P>\n<P><BR></P>\n<H3>Presenter:\u00a0</H3>\n<P>Paul Mills worked for the PwC Corporate Tax Practice for 20 years.                 "text": "The Talk:\nThis one hour talk discusses the current building and disability legislative requirements relating to access for people with disabilities in buildings.\nThis session is limited to 18 people only. Please note, this is not an online talk or webinar. It is being held in Scoresby, Victoria, Australia.\nThis is an introductory session on the topic and is suitable for architectural graduates, building surveyors, building inspectors, project managers, facility managers and anyone responsible for planning or supervising building works.\nThe Presenter:\nPresented by Lee Wilson, a disability access consultant with Melbourne Access Audits.\u00a0In early 2018 he was appointed\u00a0as a volunteer Subject Matter Expert (Disability Access) by\u00a0the Australian Building Codes Board.\u00a0\n\nLee has been actively campaigning for a universal design approach in buildings for several years and published numerous articles, a guidebook and a white paper on accessible egress concepts.\u00a0\nSeminar Timings:\n09:00 am to 09:15 am - Arrivals, networking, introductions\n09:15 am to 10:15 am - The presentation\n10:15 am to 10:30 am - Question time\nSeminar Content:\nTopics discussed will include:\n\nDisability awareness and terminology\nAn overview of the legislative framework\nThe Commonwealth Disability Discrimination Act\nDisability Standards\nState Building Act and Regulations\nThe relationship between Commonwealth and State legislation\nThe National Construction Code & Building Code of Australia\nExemptions and Concessions\nCompliance options (Performance Solutions and Deemed-to-Satisfy)\nCase studies\nQuestion time\n\nThere is an onsite cafe for those needing an expresso coffee or breakfast before the presentation.\nFAQs:\nWho should attend?\nThis seminar is suitable for people of all backgrounds and professions. It is designed as an entry-level introduction to the concept of accessibility in relation to buildings and premises.\nWhat are my transport/parking options for getting to and from the event?\nThe building is conveniently located off the Eastlink (take the BP Service Centre exit).\nThere are external car parking areas to the east of the building (off Lakeview Drive) and to the west (in front of the adjoining buildings, 35 and 37 Dalmore Drive). The best accessible car parking spaces are located in front of\u00a035 and 37 Dalmore Drive. There are no undercover accessible car parking spaces.\nIf you are coming from the city via public transport, take the train to Glen Waverley, then catch the 753 bus to\u00a0Nyadale\u00a0Drive (and then it is a 2km walk to the office building though).\nIs the building wheelchair accessible?\nYes, it is a newly constructed office building with all accessible entrances, passenger lift, left-hand and right-hand configuration accessible toilets. However, avoid the eastern external car parking area if you have any difficulties using a stair (as above, use the car park\u00a0in front of\u00a035 and 37 Dalmore Drive).\nWhere is the training room located?\nThe training room is on the ground floor of the Waterman Business Centre.\u00a0The room is called The Laneway Boardroom. The photo below is the view as you arrive at the ground floor lobby area. If you walk down past the reception area, the training room is at the end of the internal laneway. See you there.\n\n\nDoes the room have hearing augmentation provided?\nNo, there will also be no amplified sound used during the presentation. The room is a relatively small meeting room for 18 people.\nBut if you would like us to organise a portable hearing loop system please let us know we can organise this for you.\nWill any videos be open captioned?\nThere are no videos for this presentation.\n If you have any additional accessibility needs please contact our office.\u00a0\nWhat's the refund policy?\nSorry, strictly no refunds.",
